Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 116 (the Apollo 12 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Ron Burkey, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 116 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-071
	19:09 AUG. 11,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

016431,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016432,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016433,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 116.
016434,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM) 
016435,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 12.
016436,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016437,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016438,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
016439,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
016440,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 391-473
016441,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016442,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

016444,000015:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2017-01-22 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.

016450,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              in Luminary 99 than the other way around.)

016459,000030:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016460,000031:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016461,000032:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016462,000033:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016463,000034: 
016464,000035:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016465,000036: 
016466,000037:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016467,000038:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016468,000039:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016469,000040:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016470,000041: 
016471,000042:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016472,000043:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016473,000044:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016474,000045:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016475,000046:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016476,000047: 
016477,000048:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016478,000049:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016479,000050:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016480,000051:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016481,000052: 
016482,000053:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016483,000054:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016484,000055: 
016485,000056:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016486,000057: 
016487,000058:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016488,000059:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016489,000060:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016490,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016491,000062:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016492,000063: 
016493,000064:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016494,000065:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016495,000066:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016496,000067:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016497,000068: 
016498,000069:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016499,000070:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016500,000071:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016501,000072:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016502,000073:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016503,000074: 
016504,000075:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016505,000076: 
016506,000077:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016507,000078:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016508,000079:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 392 

016510,000081:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016511,000082:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016512,000083:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016513,000084:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016514,000085:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016515,000086:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016516,000087:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016517,000088:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016518,000089:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016519,000090:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016520,000091: 
016521,000092:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016522,000093:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016523,000094:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016524,000095: 
016525,000096:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016526,000097: 
016527,000098:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016528,000099:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016529,000100:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016530,000101: 
016531,000102:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016532,000103:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016533,000104:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016534,000105:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016535,000106:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016536,000107:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016537,000108:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016538,000109: 
016539,000110:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016540,000111:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016541,000112: 
016542,000113:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016543,000114: 
016544,000115:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016545,000116:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016546,000117:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016547,000118:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016548,000119: 
016549,000120:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016550,000121: 
016551,000122:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016552,000123:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016553,000124:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016554,000125:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016555,000126: 
016556,000127:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 393 

016558,000129:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016559,000130: 
016560,000131:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016561,000132: 
016562,000133:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016563,000134:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016564,000135: 
016565,000136:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016566,000137:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016567,000138:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016568,000139:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016569,000140: 
016570,000141:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016571,000142:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016572,000143: 
016573,000144:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016574,000145:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016575,000146:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016576,000147:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016577,000148: 
016578,000149:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016579,000150:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016580,000151: 
016581,000152:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016582,000153:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016583,000154: 
016584,000155:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016585,000156: 
016586,000157:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016587,000158:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016588,000159:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016589,000160:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016590,000161: 
016591,000162:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016592,000163:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016593,000164: 
016594,000165:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016595,000166:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016596,000167: 
016597,000168:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016598,000169:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016599,000170:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016600,000171: 
016601,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016602,000173: 
016603,000174:                                                                                                  #  ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016604,000175:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 394 

016606,000177:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016607,000178:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016608,000179: 
016609,000180:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016610,000181: 
016611,000182:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016612,000183: 
016613,000184:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016614,000185:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016615,000186:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
016616,000187:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016617,000188:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016618,000189:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016619,000190:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016620,000191:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016621,000192:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016622,000193:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016623,000194:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016624,000195:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016625,000196:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016626,000197:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016627,000198:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
016628,000199:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016629,000200:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016630,000201:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016631,000202:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016632,000203:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016633,000204:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016634,000205:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016635,000206:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016636,000207:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016637,000208:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13, C RELAYS
016638,000209:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016639,000210:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016640,000211:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016641,000212:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016642,000213:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016643,000214:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016644,000215:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016645,000216:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016646,000217:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016647,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016648,000219: 
016649,000220:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016650,000221: 
016651,000222:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016652,000223:

016654,000225: 
016655,000226:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
016656,000227:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
016657,000228:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET      =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
016658,000229: 
016659,000230:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
016660,000231:                                                                                                  #  WDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
016661,000232:                                                                                                  #  DECRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
016662,000233:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG      =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
016663,000234: 
016664,000235:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET      =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
016665,000236:                                                                                                  #  CHAR          =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
016666,000237:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
016667,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
016668,000239: 
016669,000240:                                                                                                  #  SGNON         =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
016670,000241:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
016671,000242:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
016672,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016673,000244: 
016674,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
016675,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
016676,000247:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016677,000248:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016678,000249:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016679,000250:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
016680,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016681,000252:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016682,000253:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMIN+1.
016683,000254:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016684,000255:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
016685,000256: 
016686,000257:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016687,000258: 
016688,000259:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
016689,000260: 
016690,000261:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT         =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016691,000262:                                                                                                  #  INREL         =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X, Y, Z, REG)
016692,000263: 
016693,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM      =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
016694,000265:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR         =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
016695,000266:

016707,000278:                                                                                                  #  TEM4          ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
016708,000279:                                                                                                  #  LSTPTR        =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY

016716,000287:                                                                                                  #  NOUNADD       =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016717,000288: 
016718,000289:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016719,000290:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016720,000291:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016721,000292:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016722,000293:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016723,000294:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016724,000295:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016725,000296:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016726,000297:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016727,000298: 
016728,000299:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016729,000300: 
016730,000301:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016731,000302: 
016732,000303:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016733,000304:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016734,000305:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016735,000306:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016736,000307:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016737,000308:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016738,000309: 
016739,000310:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016740,000311: 
016741,000312:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT        ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016742,000313:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016743,000314:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016744,000315:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION

016751,000322:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016752,000323:

Page 397 

016754,000325:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016755,000326:                                                                                                  #  0             10000
016756,000327:                                                                                                  #  1             00001
016757,000328:                                                                                                  #  9             01001
016758,000329:                                                                                                  #  VERB          10001
016759,000330:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES     10010
016760,000331:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE      11001
016761,000332:                                                                                                  #  +             11010
016762,000333:                                                                                                  #  -             11011
016763,000334:                                                                                                  #  ENTER         11100
016764,000335:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR         11110
016765,000336:                                                                                                  #  NOUN          11111
016766,000337: 
016767,000338:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016768,000339:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016769,000340:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016770,000341:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016771,000342:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016772,000343:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016773,000344: 
016774,000345:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016775,000346:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016776,000347:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016777,000348:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016778,000349:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016779,000350:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016780,000351: 
016781,000352:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016782,000353: 
016783,000354:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016784,000355:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016785,000356:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016786,000357:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016787,000358:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016788,000359:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016789,000360:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016790,000361:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016791,000362:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016792,000363:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016793,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016794,000365: 
016795,000366:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016796,000367: 
016797,000368:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016798,000369:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016799,000370:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016800,000371:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016801,000372:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016802,000373:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 398 

016804,000375:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016805,000376:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016806,000377:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016807,000378:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016808,000379:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016809,000380:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016810,000381:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016811,000382:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016812,000383:

017233,000804:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION. HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017234,000805:                                                                                                  #  DATA. THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0,- FOR HIGHER
017235,000806:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017236,000807: 
017237,000808:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017238,000809:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017239,000810:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

017524,001095:

Page 414 

017526,001097:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
017527,001098:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017528,001099:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017529,001100:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
017530,001101:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017531,001102:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017532,001103: 
017533,001104:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017534,001105:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017535,001106: 
017536,001107:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017537,001108: 
017538,001109:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017539,001110:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017540,001111:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017541,001112: 
017542,001113:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017543,001114:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017544,001115:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017545,001116:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017546,001117:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017547,001118:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017548,001119: 
017549,001120:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017550,001121:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017551,001122:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017552,001123:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017553,001124:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017554,001125: 
017555,001126:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017556,001127:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017557,001128:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017558,001129:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017559,001130:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017560,001131:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017561,001132:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017562,001133:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017563,001134: 
017564,001135:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017565,001136:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017566,001137:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017567,001138: 
017568,001139:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017569,001140:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017570,001141: 
017571,001142:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017572,001143:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017573,001144:

Page 415 

017575,001146:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017576,001147:

018125,001696:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
018126,001697:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018127,001698:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018128,001699:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO .  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018129,001700:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018130,001701:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

018154,001725:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
018155,001726:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE  OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE
018156,001727:                                                                                                  #  CADR  2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA  3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL

018721,002292:

Page 439 

018723,002294:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018724,002295:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018725,002296:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018726,002297:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018727,002298:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018728,002299: 
018729,002300:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018730,002301:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018731,002302:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018732,002303:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018733,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018734,002305:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018735,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018736,002307: 
018737,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018738,002309:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018739,002310:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018740,002311: 
018741,002312:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018742,002313:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018743,002314: 
018744,002315:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018745,002316:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018746,002317: 
018747,002318:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018872,002443:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018873,002444:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018874,002445:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018875,002446:                                                                                                  #  
018876,002447:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018877,002448: 
018878,002449:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018879,002450:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018880,002451:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018881,002452: 
018882,002453:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018883,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018884,002455:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018885,002456: 
018886,002457: 41,3361           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018887,002458: 41,3362           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018888,002459: 41,3363           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018889,002460: 41,3364           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018890,002461: 41,3365           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018891,002462: 41,3366           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018892,002463: 41,3367           03371                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018893,002464: 41,3370           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB                              
018894,002465:
