019313,002884:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
019314,002885:

Page 452 

019316,002887: 
019317,002888:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019318,002889: 
019319,002890:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019320,002891: 
019321,002892:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019322,002893:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019323,002894:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019324,002895:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019325,002896: 
019326,002897:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019327,002898:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019328,002899:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019329,002900: 
019330,002901:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019331,002902:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019332,002903:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019333,002904:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019334,002905:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019335,002906:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019336,002907:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019337,002908:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019338,002909:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019339,002910:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019340,002911:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019341,002912: 
019342,002913: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019343,002914: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019344,002915: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019345,002916: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019346,002917: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019347,002918: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019348,002919: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019349,002920: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019350,002921: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019351,002922: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019352,002923: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019353,002924: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019354,002925: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019355,002926: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019356,002927: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019357,002928: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019358,002929: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019359,002930: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019360,002931: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019361,002932: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019362,002933: 
019363,002934: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019364,002935:

Page 453 

019366,002937:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019367,002938:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019368,002939:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019369,002940:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019370,002941:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019371,002942: 
019372,002943:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019373,002944:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019374,002945:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019375,002946: 
019376,002947:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019377,002948:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019378,002949: 
019379,002950:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019380,002951:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019381,002952:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019382,002953:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019383,002954:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019384,002955: 
019385,002956:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019386,002957:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019387,002958:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019388,002959:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019389,002960: 
019390,002961:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019391,002962:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019392,002963:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019393,002964:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019394,002965:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019395,002966:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019396,002967:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019397,002968: 
019398,002969:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019399,002970:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019400,002971: 
019401,002972:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019402,002973:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019403,002974: 
019404,002975:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019405,002976:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019406,002977: 
019407,002978:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019408,002979:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019409,002980:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019410,002981:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019411,002982:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019412,002983:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019413,002984:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019414,002985: 
019415,002986:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 454 

019417,002988:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019418,002989:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019419,002990:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019420,002991:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019421,002992:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019422,002993:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019423,002994:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019424,002995:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019425,002996:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019426,002997: 
019427,002998:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019428,002999:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019429,003000: 
019430,003001:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019431,003002: 
019432,003003:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019433,003004:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019434,003005:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019435,003006:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019436,003007:    4157           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT

019438,003009:    4161           10000                           CCS      A

019440,003011:    4163           34753                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
019441,003012:    4164           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q

019443,003014:    4166           23021                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019444,003015:    4167           04204                           TC       KILMONON                              #  TURN ON KILL MONITOR BIT

019536,003107:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).

019539,003110:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019540,003111:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019541,003112:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019542,003113:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019543,003114:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019544,003115:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019545,003116: 
019546,003117:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019547,003118:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019548,003119:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019549,003120:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019550,003121:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019551,003122: 
019552,003123:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019553,003124:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019554,003125:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019555,003126:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019556,003127:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019557,003128:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019558,003129:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019559,003130:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019560,003131:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019561,003132:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019562,003133: 
019563,003134:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 457 

019565,003136:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019566,003137:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019567,003138:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019568,003139:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019569,003140:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019570,003141: 
019571,003142:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019572,003143:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019573,003144:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019574,003145:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019575,003146:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019576,003147:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019577,003148:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019578,003149:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019579,003150: 
019580,003151:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019581,003152: 
019582,003153:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019583,003154:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

019624,003195:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019625,003196:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.

019908,003479:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019909,003480: 
019910,003481:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019911,003482:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019912,003483:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019913,003484:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019914,003485: 
019915,003486:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019916,003487:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019917,003488:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019918,003489:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019919,003490:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019920,003491:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019921,003492:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019922,003493: 
019923,003494:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019924,003495:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019925,003496:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019926,003497:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019927,003498:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019928,003499: 
019929,003500:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019930,003501:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019931,003502:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019932,003503:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019933,003504:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019934,003505: 
019935,003506:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019936,003507:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019937,003508:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019938,003509: 
019939,003510: 
019940,003511:                                                                                                  #  .
019941,003512: 
019942,003513:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019943,003514:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019944,003515:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019945,003516:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019946,003517: 
019947,003518:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019948,003519:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019949,003520:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019950,003521:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019951,003522:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019952,003523:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 466 

019954,003525:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019955,003526: 
019956,003527:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019957,003528:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019958,003529:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019959,003530:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019960,003531:    4443           10631                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019961,003532:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019962,003533: 
019963,003534:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019964,003535:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019965,003536: 
019966,003537: 04,2631                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019967,003538: 04,2631                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019968,003539: 04,2631           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019969,003540: 04,2632           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019970,003541: 04,2633           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019971,003542: 04,2634           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019972,003543: 04,2635           30001                           CA       L                                     
019973,003544: 04,2636           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019974,003545: 04,2637           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019975,003546: 
019976,003547:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019977,003548:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019978,003549:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019979,003550:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019980,003551:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019981,003552: 
019982,003553:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019983,003554:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019984,003555:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019985,003556:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019986,003557:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019987,003558:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019988,003559:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019989,003560:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019990,003561:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019991,003562:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019992,003563:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

020148,003719:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020149,003720:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020150,003721:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020151,003722:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020152,003723:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020153,003724:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020154,003725:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
